				<script>
    if (current_selectline !== undefined && current_selectline=='') {
        console.log('redefine current_selectline');
        current_selectline='mgtv';
        current_selectlinename='芒果-VIP解析';
    }
    var linerate_data_json=LZString.decompressFromEncodedURIComponent(Cookies.get('linerate_data'));
    if (linerate_data_json === undefined || linerate_data_json.length
					<1) {
        linerate_data = [];
    } else {
        linerate_data = JSON.parse(linerate_data_json);
    }
    var guanfang = ['bilibili',
        'mgtv',
        'qiyi',
        'qq',
        'sohu',
        'youku'];

    function showlinerate(data) {
        if (guanfang.indexOf(current_selectline)===-1) {
            var s_score = 0;
            var a_score = 0;
            var h_score = 0;
            var rate_ppl = 0;
            var found_linerate=0;
            for (var line_id in data) {
                if (data[line_id]['name'] === current_selectline) {
                    found_linerate=1;
                    s4 = data[line_id][0];
                    s3 = data[line_id][1];
                    s2 = data[line_id][2];
                    s1 = data[line_id][3];
                    a3 = data[line_id][4];
                    a2 = data[line_id][5];
                    a1 = data[line_id][6];
                    h3 = data[line_id][7];
                    h2 = data[line_id][8];
                    h1 = data[line_id][9];
                    s_score = ((Number(s4) * 5 + Number(s3) * 4 + Number(s2) * 2 + 5) / (Number(s1) + Number(s2) + Number(s3) + Number(s4) + 1)) / 5 * 100;
                    a_score = ((Number(a3) * 5 + Number(a2) * 3 + Number(a1) + 5) / (Number(a1) + Number(a2) + Number(a3) + 1)) / 5 * 100;
                    h_score = ((Number(h3) * 5 + Number(h2) * 3 + Number(h1) + 5) / (Number(h1) + Number(h2) + Number(h3) + 1)) / 5 * 100;
                    rate_ppl = Number(s4) + Number(s3) + Number(s2) + Number(s1);
                }
            }
            if (found_linerate==1) {
                linescore = $('#line-score');
                $('a[data-lineid='+current_selectline+']').parent().parent().next().after(linescore);
                $('#line-score').removeClass('uk-hidden');
                $('#clinename').text(current_selectlinename);
                $('#rateppl').text('来自'+rate_ppl+'人反馈');
                showratestar(s_score,'#p_speed','#t_speed');
                showratestar(a_score,'#p_ad','#t_ad');
                showratestar(h_score,'#p_hd','#t_hd');
            } else {
                if ($('#line-score').hasClass('uk-hidden') === false) {
                    $('#line-score').addClass('uk-hidden');
                }
            }
        } else {
            if ($('#line-score').hasClass('uk-hidden') === false) {
                $('#line-score').addClass('uk-hidden');
            }
        }
    }

    function aftergetlinerate(data) {
        linerate_data = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(data));
        Cookies.set('linerate_data',LZString.compressToEncodedURIComponent(JSON.stringify(linerate_data)),{ expires: 3/24,path:'/'});
        showlinerate(linerate_data);
    }

    function showratestar(score,starProgressid,starTextid) {
        starProgress = $(starProgressid);
        starProgress.empty();
        starText = $(starTextid);
        console.log(starProgressid+' score:'+score);
        fullStars = Math.floor(score / 10);
        halfStar = (score) % 10 >= 5 ? 1 : 0;
        console.log('fullStars:'+fullStars);
        console.log('half:'+halfStar);
        for (let i = 0; i < fullStars; i++) {
            starProgress.append('
						<i class="fas fa-star"></i>');
        }
        if (halfStar) {
            starProgress.append('
						<i class="fas fa-star-half-stroke"></i>');
        }
        for (let i = fullStars + halfStar; i < 10; i++) {
            starProgress.append('
						<i class="far fa-star fa-regular"></i>');
        }
        starText.text(score.toFixed(1));
    }

    function line_select_event(lineid,linename) {
        current_selectline = lineid;
        current_selectlinename = linename;
        //console.log('current line:'+current_selectline);
        if (linerate_data !== undefined && linerate_data.length
						<1) {
            $.ajax({
                url: 'https://kpdata.ethersaga.online/kapi/get_linegetrate_p',
                dataType: 'jsonp',
                jsonp: 'callback',
                jsonpCallback:"aftergetlinerate",
                success: function(data) {
                    //console.log('linerate fetch success'+JSON.stringify(data));
                },
                error:function(){
                    console.log('linerate fetch failed');
                },
                timeout: 3000
            });
        } else {
            //console.log('switch line:'+current_selectline);
            showlinerate(linerate_data);
        }

    }

    $(function() {
        $('.line-select').on('click', function() {
            line_select_event($(this).data('lineid'),$(this).data('linename'));
        });
        if  ($('#line-score').length > 0) {
            line_select_event(current_selectline,current_selectlinename);
        }
    });


						</script>
